*framework.PodsToActivate) *fwk.Status {\\n277: \\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\\n278: \\n279: \\tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\\n280: \\n281: \\tif sched.nominatedNodeNameForExpectationEnabled when Pods are rejected at specific extension points, and Permit is the last one in the scheduling/binding cycle.\\n320: \\t// If a Pod fails on PreBind or Bind, it should be moved to BackoffQ for retry.\\n321: \\t//\\n322: \\t// We can call Done() here because\\n323: \\t// we can free the cluster events stored in the scheduling queue sooner, which is worth for busy clusters memory consumption scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\\n350: \\n351: \\t// At the end of a successful binding cycle, move up Pods if needed.\\n352: \\tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\\n353: no longer consumed.\\n356: \\t}\\n357: \\n358: \\treturn nil\\n359: }\\n360: \\n361: func (sched *Scheduler) handleBindingCycleError(\\n362: \\tctx context.Context,\\n363: \\tstate // If it fails, it will return a FitError with reasons.\\n426: func (sched *Scheduler) schedulePod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state fwk.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) (result error) {\\n488: \\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\\n489: \\tdiagnosis := framework.Diagnosis{\\n490: \\t\\tNodeToStatus: framework.NewDefaultNodeToStatus(),\\n491: \\t}\\n492: \\n493: \\tallNodes, \\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\\n713: }\\n714: \\n715: // numFeasibleNodesToFind returns the number of feasible nodes that once found, the scheduler stops\\n716: // its search for more feasible nodes.\\n717: func (sched *Scheduler) numFeasibleNodesToFind(percentageOfNodesToScore *int32, numAllNodes int32) (numNodes int32) {\\n718: \\tif numAllNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\\n719: \\t\\treturn numAllNodes\\n720: \\t}\\n721: \\n722: \\t// Use profile percentageOfNodesToScore if it's set. *Scheduler) findNodesThatFitPod(ctx context.Context, schedFramework framework.Framework, state fwk.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) ([]fwk.NodeInfo, framework.Diagnosis, string, fwk.PodSignature, error) \t}\n712: \treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n713: }\n714: \n715: // numFeasibleNodesToFind returns the number of feasible nodes that once found, the scheduler stops\n716: // its search for more feasible nodes.\n717: func (sched *Scheduler) numFeasibleNodesToFind(percentageOfNodesToScore *int32, numAllNodes int32) (numNodes int32) {\n718: \tif numAllNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\n719: \t\treturn []fwk.Extender, pod *v1.Pod, feasibleNodes []fwk.NodeInfo, statuses *framework.NodeToStatus) ([]fwk.NodeInfo, error) {\n746: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n747: \n748: \t// Extenders are called sequentially.\n749: \t// Nodes in original feasibleNodes can be excluded in one extender, and pass on to the next\n750: \t// extender in a decreasing manner.\n751: \tfor _, extender := range extenders eventually improve preemption efficiency.\n762: \t\t// Note: users are recommended to configure the extenders that may return UnschedulableAndUnresolvable\n763: \t\t// status ahead of others.\n764: the nodes by running the score plugins,\n792: // which return a score for each node from the call to RunScorePlugins().\n793: // The scores from each plugin are added together to make the score for that node, then\n794: // any extenders are run as well.\n795: // All scores are finally combined (added) to get the total weighted scores of all nodes\n796: func prioritizeNodes(\n797: \tctx context.Context,\n798: \textenders []fwk.Extender,\n799: \tschedFramework framework.Framework,\n800: \tstate fwk.CycleState,\n801: \tpod *v1.Pod,\n802: \tnodes []fwk.NodeInfo,\n803: ) ([]fwk.NodePluginScores, error) {\n804: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n805: \t// If no priority configs are provided, then all nodes will have a score of one.\n806: \t// This is required to generate the priority list in the required format\n807: \tif len(extenders) == 0 && !schedFramework.HasScorePlugins() {\n808: \t\tresult := make([]fwk.NodePluginScores, 0, len(nodes))\n809: \t\tfor i \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"plugin\", pluginScore.Name, \"node\", nodeScore.Name, \"score\", pluginScore.Score)\n836: \t\t\t}\n837: \t\t}\n838: \t}\n839: \n840: \tif len(extenders) != 0 && nodes != nil {\n841: \t\t// allNodeExtendersScores has all extenders scores for all nodes.\n842: \t\t// It is keyed with node name.\n843: \t\tallNodeExtendersScores := make(map[string]*fwk.NodePluginScores, \t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Failed to run extender's priority function. No score given by this extender.\", \"error\", err, \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"extender\", extenders[extIndex].Name())\n861: \t\t\t\t\treturn\n862: \t\t\t\t}\n863: \t\t\t\tmu.Lock()\n864:
